Merging K Sorted Lists Oracle ^99kFav53

You are given an array of k linked-lists lists, each linked-list is sorted in ascending order. ^MchfarIQ

Merge all the linked-lists into one sorted linked-list and return it. ^4ZmJvOld

Input: lists = [[1,4,5],[1,3,4],[2,6]] ^ojeiB4UW

Output: [1,1,2,3,4,4,5,6] ^3xeJFb4l

merging them into one sorted list: ^yc3vKyW8

1->1->2->3->4->4->5->6 ^GFgIcGY7

Class Node;
    int vale
    Node next ^WI9m3zA8

prev = none
cu = head
loop cu is not null:
    next = cu.next
    cu.next = prev
    prev = cu
    cu = next
head = prev

slow = head
fast = head

while fast and fast.next is not null
    slow = slow.next
    fast = fast.next.next
    if slow == fast
        return True ^jGIyMKjw

Merge Sort Algorithm ^4wm311UT

dummy = Node(0)
current = dummy
while l1 and l2:
    if l1.val < l2.val
        current.next = l1
        l1 = l1.next
    else:
        current.next = l2
        l2 = l2.next
    current = current.next
# add left over
current.next = l1 or l2
return dummy.next ^ps2Db6dc

lists = []

while lists.length > 1
    ans = []
    for i in range(0, list.lenght, 2)
        list1 = lists[i]
        list2 = lists[i+1] # condition, if its available
        res = mergelist(list1, list2)
        ans.add(res)
    
    lists = ans

return list[0]
